<div id="review_2934618507" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2934618507" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2934618507?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2934618507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2204293642686055473"><b>uhh, i feel scammed. why had the author published this as the companion novel?! this would’ve made for a better first book in the series!!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>✨ 3.5 <i>"I LOVE TO HATE YOU"</i> stars ✨</b>
</blockquote><br/>i'm so glad that we get to meet more characters in this book as well as see different sides of the existing ones we’ve already known from the first book. it’s not necessarily that we see their good sides. it’s that we see them from a different angle and are able to understand them more. i know this is kind of the whole poi</span>
  <span id="freeText2204293642686055473" style="display:none"><b>uhh, i feel scammed. why had the author published this as the companion novel?! this would’ve made for a better first book in the series!!</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>✨ 3.5 <i>"I LOVE TO HATE YOU"</i> stars ✨</b>
</blockquote><br />i'm so glad that we get to meet more characters in this book as well as see different sides of the existing ones we’ve already known from the first book. it’s not necessarily that we see their good sides. it’s that we see them from a different angle and are able to understand them more. i know this is kind of the whole point of a companion novel. (<i>duhh!!</i>) what i’m saying is that this book has managed to make me hate these characters less.<br /><br /><b>see horny jared, his <i>halfassed</i> apologies, and him trying to get to know the word "commitment", as well as his lesson on "how to (not) be a bitter person" here.</b><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[i still haven’t changed my mind about jared (and most of the other characters really). while i appreciate that i get to glimpse more into his childhood and see how his “broken home” situation has affected him as a person, i also feel like most of the time jared just keeps constantly justifying his misdemeanor towards tate with how he’s been treated by his family. i don’t like his “no one else gets to mess with her unless it’s me” mentality. he has the audacity to claim that he’s not like those other <i>cocksuckers</i> who harass women while he’s practically doing the same thing to tate.<br /><br /><blockquote><b><i>“now, i could go on about mommy didn’t love me and daddy hit me, but who doesn’t have a story, right?” i asked. “there are times when we can blame a situation on others, but we own our reactions to them. there comes a point where we are the ones responsible for our choices and excuses don’t carry weight anymore.”</i></b></blockquote><br />other than persistently being on the move to plot tate’s demise, being in jared’s head also feels like seeing inside the brain of a horny twelve year old who’s just found his first sport illustrated magazine. he keeps making comments about tate’s hair, eyes, “athletic” body, the clothes she wears, and pointing out how all those things get him hard. on a brighter note, i really love all of the interactions he has with tate’s dad, his brother jaxon, and his mother. his father can go to hell!! i’m also less annoyed with his friendship with madoc. the whole ordeal with kc, that’s still my most disliked thing about him. oh and the speech at the end of the book, that’s nice. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b><u>overall thoughts</u>:</b><br /><br />i enjoyed this book better than the original first book. i would have jumped straight into this one had i known it existed prior to my reading of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2937039818?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">bully</a>. there are more characters. tate’s dad being my most favorite one even though he only appears briefly. i also think the characters’ development is better in this one. more things are also happening in this book. it still have some key events from tate’s book that are now being shown through jared’s pov. sometimes those scenes feel repetitive and pointless bcs jared’s either thinking about antagonizing tate or having “sexual” reactions bcs of her. i really like the additional scenes, the ones that have no involvement of tate. last but not least, this book is definitely a whole lot steamier compare to the first one.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(read in audiobook format)</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2204293642686055473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_824059816" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/824059816" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/824059816?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18260742-until-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer824059816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3610944070095875018">4.5 ★'s<br/><br/>If you liked <i>Bully</i>, you will love <i>Until You</i>! This story dot's all the i's and crosses all the t's and leaves ~<i>almost</i>~ every question answered. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Tate - I'm still enchanted by her and maybe a little more so just hearing about her from Jared's POV. I love how she keeps him on his toes. <br/><br/>• Jared - ahhhh...it was nice getting those badly needed answers. I now understand him so much better.<br/><br/>• Tate's Dad - I love how he was with Jared. <i>Exactly</i> what he needed. And his secret was so sad! </span>
  <span id="freeText3610944070095875018" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s<br><br>If you liked <i>Bully</i>, you will love <i>Until You</i>! This story dot's all the i's and crosses all the t's and leaves ~<i>almost</i>~ every question answered. <br><br><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Tate - I'm still enchanted by her and maybe a little more so just hearing about her from Jared's POV. I love how she keeps him on his toes. <br><br>• Jared - ahhhh...it was nice getting those badly needed answers. I now understand him so much better.<br><br>• Tate's Dad - I love how he was with Jared. <i>Exactly</i> what he needed. And his secret was so sad! <br><br>• Jared's sexual escapades - I liked getting the inside scoop!<br><br>• I also liked knowing about him and K.C. <br><br>• Henry!<br><br>• Loved what happened to Nate and Piper - especially Piper!<br><br>• Jaxon - I loved how PD got things going with him....I think I have a good clue who he will be with.<br><br>• We get an excerpt for Madoc's book. Can't wait to find out more about this piercing! ;)<br><br>• Annnd...PD lets us know that we will get more updates on Jared and Tate in the next books. Which I know is kind of obvious but still good to hear. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389772529i/8053794.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Dislikes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Jared's Dad - I think I hate him even more!<br><br>• What happened between K.C. and Jared - I still don't like that no one has told Tate. <br><br>• Jared's mom seeing them! <br><br>• Overuse of "pinching" eyebrows about drove me nuts!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389771720i/8053754.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall:</u>
</b><br><br>I was really happy that I decided to go ahead and read this book right after reading <i>Bully</i>. It gave me such a deeper reading experience and I didn't feel like I was reading the same thing. Obviously, there are similar stories but PD manages to change things up enough that it feels fresh. I definitely would recommend reading <i>Bully</i> before this one though. Can't wait for Madoc's and Jax's books!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389912229i/8095335.jpg" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “You were my tempest, my thunder cloud, my tree in the downpour. I loved all of those things, and I loved you. But now…you’re a fucking drought. I thought that all the assholes drove German cars, but it turns out that pricks in Mustangs can still leave scars.”<br><br>♥ “Jared,” she whispered between kisses. “Something’s wrong with me. I always want more of you.”<br><br>♥ “Girlfriend isn’t enough to describe you, Tate. That term is disposable. You’re not my girlfriend, my girl, or my woman. You’re. Just. Mine.” <br><br>♥ “It wasn’t until two years later that I found something that I loved more than Henry."<br><br>♥ “Have you ever considered a nipple piercing?”</span>

<div id="review_683480386" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/683480386" />
    <a title="Jaydb" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11805349-jaydb"><img alt="Jaydb" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362102966p2/11805349.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/683480386?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jaydb" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jaydb" href="/user/show/11805349-jaydb">Jaydb</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18260742-until-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer683480386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13444246492169493839">The first chapter has been released earlier this week, and I'm telling you... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369726ra/722478.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In Bully, we get a general idea of what happened to Jared that made him the bully that he became to Tate. I just never expected that it was like THAT!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406807ra/794104.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I wanted to kill someone. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390070ra/751590.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Then we are given a peek at a day in the life of Jared Trent. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410158ra/803756.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Anyone who's read Bully knows that Jared slept around A LOT... but really reading about it from his POV was still like a bitter pill to swallow. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/>Apparent</span>
  <span id="freeText13444246492169493839" style="display:none">The first chapter has been released earlier this week, and I'm telling you... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369726ra/722478.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In Bully, we get a general idea of what happened to Jared that made him the bully that he became to Tate. I just never expected that it was like THAT!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406807ra/794104.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wanted to kill someone. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390070ra/751590.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then we are given a peek at a day in the life of Jared Trent. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410158ra/803756.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Anyone who's read Bully knows that Jared slept around A LOT... but really reading about it from his POV was still like a bitter pill to swallow. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Apparently our feisty Tate has started standing up to him just before she left for France, not when she came back a year later. LOL, what she did..!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/461180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So basically, my reactions while reading the free chapter were just different variations of "OH MY GOD". That short excerpt simply had me gaping and OMG-ing the entire time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/495109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am so excited for this book! We only saw the tip of the iceberg (about Jared) in Bully, IMO. I cannot wait to learn more about him and his experiences, how he really saw Tate, and BY GOD, I want to know the why's and what's with KC....! Even days after reading Bully, I cannot get it out of my mind<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ that bit about her leaving Jared's house at midnight really bothered me :( and Tate saw that too! and right after that Jared said something really hurtful to Tate.. :(  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>But at the end of it all, this was me:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388009ra/748342.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>:D I just cannot wait for Until You!<br><br>UPDATE: <br><br>Needless to say I've been stalking Penelope Douglas's Facebook :D her Me-Hubby convo posts are hilarious, just saying! But of course, Until You related posts are the best treats. They never fail to make my day! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431449i/865804._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431449i/865805._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13444246492169493839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/703019347?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mia" href="/user/show/22667925-mia">Mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18260742-until-you">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer703019347" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5422494261102489793"><blockquote>
  <i>Yesterday lasts forever.<br/>Tomorrow comes never.<br/><b>Until you.</b></i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563808.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Really loved this book! Bully was one of my favourite books of the year and I enjoyed this one just as much. <br/><br/>Kudos to you, Penelope Douglas, for writing a kickass companion novel –not an easy task! Although this followed the same storyline as <i>Bully</i>, it had many new scenes and I loved seeing what was going through Jared’s head throughout the book. My heart broke for him and all he had to put up with. I think anyone who was on the fence ab</span>
  <span id="freeText5422494261102489793" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>Yesterday lasts forever.<br>Tomorrow comes never.<br><b>Until you.</b></i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563808.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really loved this book! Bully was one of my favourite books of the year and I enjoyed this one just as much. <br><br>Kudos to you, Penelope Douglas, for writing a kickass companion novel –not an easy task! Although this followed the same storyline as <i>Bully</i>, it had many new scenes and I loved seeing what was going through Jared’s head throughout the book. My heart broke for him and all he had to put up with. I think anyone who was on the fence about Bully should definitely give this one a chance. Being inside Jared's head and understanding his guilt, emotional baggage and the reasons behind his asshole-ness may change your mind about him. <br><br>But more than Jared, I freaking ADORE Madoc! I’m really looking forward to his and Jax’s books. I still can’t stand KC, who I’m guessing is Jax’s love interest, but I hope to warm up to her by then. <br><br>I will always love Jared and Tate’s story, the way they grew up together and everything they mean to each other. Looking forward to reading more from this author and the next Fall Away books! <br></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_680848547" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680848547" />
    <a title="Ing" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4636302-ing"><img alt="Ing" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441753792p2/4636302.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680848547?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ing" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ing" href="/user/show/4636302-ing">Ing</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18260742-until-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680848547" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17984350744903865029">Read original review on blog: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://bit.ly/1biHhSn'>http://bit.ly/1biHhSn</a><br/><br/>You know that feeling where you crave a certain food so bad that you can literally taste that sucker and you won't be satisfied until you eat it? Once you indulge in your craving this euphoria settles on you and you feel all full and complete? Well waiting for UNTIL YOU to release and then finally reading the dang book gave me those exact same feelings. I was floating on cloud nine. I didn't think that I could love Jared more but I did after rea</span>
  <span id="freeText17984350744903865029" style="display:none">Read original review on blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1biHhSn">http://bit.ly/1biHhSn</a><br><br>You know that feeling where you crave a certain food so bad that you can literally taste that sucker and you won't be satisfied until you eat it? Once you indulge in your craving this euphoria settles on you and you feel all full and complete? Well waiting for UNTIL YOU to release and then finally reading the dang book gave me those exact same feelings. I was floating on cloud nine. I didn't think that I could love Jared more but I did after reading HIS story. Until You is book #1.5 of the Fall Away series and is the companion novel to Bully. This is told from Jared Trent's POV. I think Penelope said it best in her note from the author section, "This is NOT a retelling of Bully. This is Jared's story." Truer words have never been spoken. This was definitely Jared's book all the way. Penelope lets the readers in and took us on a roller-coaster ride full of bumps, thrills and joy. <br><br>I loved, loved, loved BULLY. I didn't always agree with how Jared treated Tate half of the time in that book. Even though he was such a jerk face I still fell in love with him in Bully. I wanted in badly inside his head. When Penelope announced that she would be writing a book from Jared's POV, I fist pumped the air and jumped up and down squealing like a 10 year old girl! Finally we'd get to hear what Jared was thinking in some places during Bully and finally we can get a better understanding how someone could turn so against and so mean towards someone who was their world and best friend.<br><br>Did Until You deliver for this fan? Fudge YES it did. That one summer spent with his father was a freaking nightmare. If I could reach in and tear Thomas Trent a new a-hole I would have. That man put Jared and his brother Jax through hell. My heart broke for the both of them. Especially Jax. I can't imagine what a nightmare it was for Jax living that whole time with a father like that. What Jared's father put him through messed him up so bad that something in Jared broke that summer. I hate that Jared turned on Tate. I wish he would have reached out to her but I get it. I totally get where his head was and how he could have flipped things into what it was. Does any of it still excuse his treatment of Tate, heck no but I get it. <br><br>As it's been stated this was definitely not a retelling of Bully. We get so much more new information in this book. We saw what Jared was up to while Tate was away. We got to see more Madoc, who is Jared's best friend and partner in crime. I can't wait for Madoc's book. Madoc is freaking funny. He's so silly and had some of the funniest lines in this book. His and Fallon's story is going to be great. That girl is going to take that boy down a notch. I totally fell in love and have a massive crush with a Tate's dad in this book. Mr. Brandt plays a bigger role in Jared's book. I love his no BS policy and how he told Jared like it is. His advice and wisdom was something Jared was missing in his life. I was so glad that he got that from Mr. Brandt. He got something he never had and respected it. Jax...oh Jax you are going to be trouble and I have a feeling you are going to make my heart break. I am so scared to know what happened to Jax. His story I have a feeling will be even more devastating. Sigh I can't wait.<br>Now let's get to K.C. who was Tate's best friend. I hated that girl so much in Bully. She broke the girl code and really hurt Tate in Bully. I wanted to pull her hair and slap her silly in Bully. I wasn't sure how Penelope would redeem her in Until You. I wanted to know how Jared could use K.C. in that way to hurt Tate and I wanted to know how K.C. could have even contemplated being with Jared and hurting Tate. I got my answers. Did it make me hate K.C. less. Yes it did. I don't love her but I like her enough now. I am hoping and don't get mad other Fall Away fans but I want to hear more about K.C. She has a story and I am hoping she gets one! :)<br><br>Tate's voice is more in the background in this book. For me I STRONGLY recommend you read Bully first before you read Until You. It will add to the experience. But her voice during Bully was very strong that even though all of this was from Jared's POV there were many times her voice was in the background in my head talking smack back to Jared. I love Tate. Seeing Tate from Jared's eye I fell in love with her more. I'm so glad to see her put Jared in his place at the end and told him like it is. Jared needed to hear that. I don't think he ever really got it until that moment or he just tried to gloss it all over in his head.<br><br>OMERGAWD!!!! I can't tell you how much I LURVED being inside Jared's head. Guys tend to be dirtier and raunchier with their thoughts. Being in Jared's head was like being allowed in a bookstore with no money limit to buy books. I was all over the place squeeeing and just falling in love with him and was greedy. I knew this book was going to be HOT because Penelope teased us. But boy howdy freaking holy oh...that boy was mind f--king Tate all over! Several times I was cuing the porno jingle in my head while reading. Oh how I loved it. Besides the sexier scenes just seeing the more emotional moments through Jared's eye was refreshing. I felt like I was reading a whole new book and feeling all those same emotions I felt while reading Bully. There was a very touching moment with Jared and his mom. It was a very poignant moment between two people who have drifted apart so much. I'm glad the rift is slowly closing. <br><br>Fans of Bully will not be disappointed with Until You. Penelope Douglas delivers big time and meets all the expectations that this fan had for Until You. Being inside Jared's head was one crazy emotional roller coaster ride. With the addition of Until You, Penelope has become an author I trust and will automatically buy anything this woman writes. I recommend this series with all my heart. If I could marry this series and have a family with it I so totally would! :)<br><br>************************<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386395911i/7355755._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo UY_Teaser4_zps7d8567ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************************<br><br>One of the characters that shined in this book! Totally have mad crush on Tate's dad! I heart you James Brandt!!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386395911i/7355756.jpg" alt=" photo UY_Teaser5_zps432eb44c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************************<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386395911i/7355757._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo UY_Teaser3_zpscf5956bf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************************<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386395911i/7355758._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo UY_Teaser2_zps23daa3d4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************************<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385439929i/7149669.jpg" alt=" photo UntilYouTeaser_zps9c0228b9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************************<br><br>Horrible book hangover! Jared &amp; Tate fans will not be disappointed. Jared I love you even more than before. This was me the whole time reading the book! Full review to come soon.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385083530i/7062644.jpg" alt=" photo child-very-excited1_zps6a010544.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aMr8kmc238IZps/ftLCiW+yGMw5DWb8PzHw+yvxQQT95iZG+ZzgrWbZpj5LlVmNNOlxocscsUeHBhry3W/jwDw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Km4clD7UNNMVY9kGart3TqMwZNBXPTyvyrMuLlKxKJ07LXG4PtrASLqsmUs7XbZYdeo/rNNI0kHHSaxT9RmZrQ==')})
  }
